### Response: Question: A coder has 1000 followers on Twitter. He gains 100 followers every day. How many followers will he have in 5 days? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A 20-year-old man is 66 inches tall.  His 10-year-old brother is 2/3 his height.  How tall is the 10-year-old in feet? Solution: def solution():

    return result

### Instruction:
Write one math word problem and Python code with a commented out step-by-step
### Response: Question: A baker is making a 3-layer cake. The first layer is 10 inches in diameter. The second layer is 8 inches in diameter. The third layer is 6 inches in diameter. What is the volume of the cake? Solution: def solution():
    #The first layer is 10 inches in diameter
    layer_1_diameter = 10
    #The second layer is 8 inches in diameter
    layer_2_diameter = 8
    #The third layer is 6 inches in diameter
    layer_3_diameter = 6
    #The height of each layer is 4 inches
    layer_height = 4
    #The volume of a cylinder is pi * radius^2 * height
    #The radius of the first layer is 10/2 = <<10/2=5>>5 inches
    layer_1_radius = 5
    layer_1_volume = 3.14 * (layer_1_radius ** 2) * layer_height
    #The radius of the second layer is 8/2 = <<8/2=4>>4 inches
    layer_2_radius = 4
    layer_2_volume = 3.14 * (layer_2_radius ** 2) * layer_height
    #The radius of the third layer is 6/2 = <<6/2=3>>3 inches
    layer_3_radius = 3
    layer_3_volume = 3.14 * (layer_3_radius ** 2) * layer_height
    #The total volume is
    result = layer_1_volume + layer_2_volume + layer_3_volume
    return result

### Response: Question: The soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are defenders. The rest of the players are goalies. How many goalies are there? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 are defenders
    players_defenders = 6
    #The rest are goalies
    players_goalies = players_total - players_forwards - players_defenders
    result = players_goalies
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-pound sack of apples costs $22. A 20-pound sack of apples costs $44. How much will 30 pounds of apples cost? Solution: def solution():
    #10 pounds of apples cost $22
    apples_10_pounds = 22
    #20 pounds of apples cost $44
    apples_20_pounds = 44
    #The answer is
    result = (apples_20_pounds - apples_10_pounds) / 10 + apples_10_pounds
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-pound bag of apples has 40 apples. How many 10-pound bags of apples does it take to have 120 apples? Solution: def solution():

    #120 apples / 40 apples per 10 pounds = <<120/40=3>>3 10-pound bags of apples

    return result

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Hotel has 240 rooms. 70% of the rooms are occupied. How many rooms are unoccupied? Solution: def solution():
    #The hotel has 240 rooms
    rooms = 240
    #70% of the rooms are occupied
    occupancy_percent = 70
    #The answer is
    result = rooms * (1 - occupancy_percent / 100)
    return result

### Response: Question: The gym has 100 towels. 20% of the towels are white. 50% of the towels are blue. The rest of the towels are green. How many towels are green? Solution: def solution():
    #20% of the towels are white
    white_towels = 0.2 * 100
    #50% of the towels are blue
    blue_towels = 0.5 * 100
    #The rest are green
    green_towels = 100 - white_towels - blue_towels
    return green_towels

### Response: Question: A 1
### Response: Question: A 20-pound box of oranges has 280 oranges. A 10-pound box of oranges has 140 oranges. How many oranges can you get for $10? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-pound box of oranges has 280 oranges
    oranges_20_pounds = 280
    #A 10-pound box of oranges has 140 oranges
    oranges_10_pounds = 140
    #The 20-pound box costs $20
    cost_20_pounds = 20
    #The 10-pound box costs $10
    cost_10_pounds = 10
    #The 20-pound box has
    oranges_20_pounds_per_dollar = oranges_20_pounds / cost_20_pounds
    #oranges per dollar. The 10-pound box has
    oranges_10_pounds_per_dollar = oranges_10_pounds / cost_10_pounds
    #oranges per dollar. The average is
    oranges_per_dollar = (oranges_20_pounds_per_dollar + oranges_10_pounds_per_dollar) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = oranges_per_dollar * 10
    return result

### Response: Question: A cafeteria has 200 hamburgers. It sells 90 hamburgers at lunch and 120 hamburgers at dinner. How many hamburgers are left? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A candy store sells 12 chocolate bars and 8 bags of gummy bears. Each chocolate bar costs $2.50 and each bag of gummy bears costs $3. The candy store then buys 3 bags of licorice and 4 bags of jelly beans. Each bag of licorice costs $2 and each bag of jelly beans costs $1.50. How much money did the candy store spend? Solution: def solution():
    #The candy store sold 12 chocolate bars
    chocolate_bars = 12
    #Each chocolate bar costs $2.50
    chocolate_bar_cost = 2.5
    #The candy store sold 8 bags of gummy bears
    gummy_bears = 8
    #Each bag of gummy bears costs $3
    gummy_bear_cost = 3
    #The candy store then bought 3 bags of licorice
    licorice = 3
    #Each bag of licorice costs $2
    licorice_cost = 2
    #The candy store bought 4 bags of jelly beans
    jelly_beans = 4
    #Each bag of jelly beans costs $1.50
    jelly_bean_cost = 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = (chocolate_bars * chocolate_bar_cost) + (gummy_bears * gummy_bear_cost) - (licorice * licorice_cost) - (jelly_beans * jelly_bean_cost)
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces. 20% of the weight is from the packaging. How much does the soap itself weigh? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_weight = 4
    #20% of the weight is from the packaging
    packaging_weight = soap_weight * 0.2
    #The answer is
    result = soap_weight - packaging_weight
    return result

### Response: Question: A theater has 200 seats. 40% of the seats are occupied by men and 10% by children. The rest are occupied by women. How many women are in the theater? Solution: def solution():
    #The total number of people in a theater is 200
    people_total = 200
    #40% of the people are men
    men_percent = 0.4
    #10% are children
    children_percent = 0.1
    #The rest are women
    women_percent = 1 - men_percent - children_percent
    #The number of women is
    women = people_total * women_percent
    return women

### Response: Question: The soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards, 6 are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many players are midfielders and defenders? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 are midfielders
    players_midfielders = 6
    #The rest are defenders
    players_defenders = players_total - players_forwards - players_midfielders
    #The answer is
    result = players_midfielders + players_defenders
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces.  A bottle of detergent weighs 10 ounces.  A bottle of bleach weighs 8 ounces.  How much do 10 cakes of soap, 5 boxes of soap powder, 3 bottles of detergent, and 2 bottles of bleach weigh? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces
    soap_powder_weight = 16
    #A bottle of detergent weighs 10 ounces
    detergent_weight = 10
    #A bottle of bleach weighs 8 ounces
    bleach_weight = 8
    #10 cakes of soap weigh
    soap_cake_total = soap_cake_weight * 10
    #5 boxes of soap powder weigh
    soap_powder_total = soap_powder_weight * 5
    #3 bottles of detergent weigh
    detergent_total = detergent_weight * 3
    #2 bottles of bleach weigh
    bleach_total = bleach_weight * 2
    #The answer is
    result = soap_cake_total + soap_powder_total + detergent_total + bleach_total
    return result

### Response: Question: A baker is making a cake. The cake's recipe calls for 4.5 cups of flour. The baker has 1.5 cups of white flour and 2.5 cups of whole wheat flour. How many more cups of flour does the baker need? Solution: def solution():
    #The cake calls for 4.5 cups of flour
    flour_needed = 4.5
    #The baker has 1.5 cups of white flour
    flour_white = 1.5
    #The baker has 2.5 cups of whole wheat flour
    flour_wheat = 2.5
    #The baker has a total of
    flour_total = flour_white + flour_wheat
    #The baker needs
    result = flour_needed - flour_total
    return result
Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropri
### Response: Question: A baker has 200 muffins. He sells 1/4 of the muffins in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining muffins in the afternoon. How many muffins does he have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker has 200 muffins
    muffins = 200
    #1/4 of the muffins were sold in the morning
    muffins_sold_morning = muffins / 4
    #1/2 of the remaining muffins were sold in the afternoon
    muffins_sold_afternoon = (muffins - muffins_sold_morning) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = muffins - muffins_sold_morning - muffins_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: 123456789 is a 9-digit number. If you add the 1st, 3rd, and 5th digits, you get 1 + 3 + 5 = <<1+3+5=9>>9. If you add the 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 7th digits, you get 2 + 4 + 6 + 7 = <<2+4+6+7=19>>19. If you add the 8th and 9th digits, you get 8 + 9 = <<8+9=17>>17. The sum of all the digits is 9 + 19 + 17 = <<9+19+17=45>>45. What is the 8th digit of 123456789? Solution: def solution():
    #The 8th and 9th digits sum to 17
    digit_8_9 = 17
    #The 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 7th digits sum to 19
    digit_2_4_6_7 = 19
    #The 1st, 3rd, and 5th digits sum to 9
    digit_1_3_5 = 9
    #The sum of all the digits is 45
    digit_sum = 45
    #The 8th digit is
    result = digit_8_9 - 9
    return result

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards, 8 are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many players are defenders? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players = 24
    #12 are forwards
    forwards = 12
    #8 are midfielders
    midfielders = 8
    #The rest are defenders
    defenders = players - forwards - midfielders
    return defenders

### Response: Question: A baker has 240 muffins. She sells 1/3 of the muffins in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining muffins in the afternoon. How many muffins does she have left? Solution: def solution():

    return result

### Response: Question: A baker bakes 200 loaves of bread. He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread does he have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker bakes 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked / 2
    #He has
    loaves_left_after_morning = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning
    #loaves left after the morning.
    #He sells 1/2 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = loaves_left_after_morning / 2
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_left_after_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  Hotel Maid Nicole has to make 1000 cakes of soap.  She has a 55-gallon drum of soap base, which weighs 440 pounds.  How many ounces of fragrance and coloring does she need to add to the drum of soap base to make her 1000 cakes of soap? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #Hotel Maid Nicole has to make 1000 cakes of soap
    num_cakes = 1000
    #She has a 55-gallon drum of soap base, which weighs 440 pounds
    soap_base_weight = 440
    #A pound is 16 ounces
    pounds_to_ounces = 16
    #The total weight of the cakes of soap she wants to make is
    soap_cake_weight * num_cakes = 4 * 1000 = <<4*1000=4000>>4000
    #The total weight of the soap base is
    soap_base_weight * pounds_to_ounces = 440 * 16 = <<440*16=7040>>7040
    #The difference is
    result = 7040 - 4000 = <<7040-4000=3040>>3040
    return result

### Response: Question: A toy car can drive 20 miles on a full battery. The toy car's battery lasts for 2 hours. How many miles can the toy car drive in 4 hours? Solution: def solution():
    #The toy car can drive 20 miles on a full battery
    miles_per_battery = 20
    #The battery lasts for 2 hours
    hours_per_battery = 2
    #4 hours is 4/2 = <<4/2=2>>2 batteries
    num_batteries = 4 / hours_per_battery
    #The answer is
    result = miles_per_battery * num_batteries
    return result

### Response: Question: 20000 people live in a large town. 60% of the population are men. How many men live in the town? Solution: def solution():

    population = 20000
    #60% of the population are men
    men_percent = 60
    #40% of the population are women
    women_percent = 100 - men_percent
    #60% of the population are women
    men = population * men_percent / 100
    #The answer is
    result = men
    return result

### Response: Question: A gym can hold 200 people. The gym was 60% full. 100 more people came in. The gym was then 80% full. How many people can the gym hold? Solution: def solution():
    #The gym was 60% full
    gym_full_60 = 0.6
    #100 more people came in
    people_came_in = 100
    #The gym was then 80% full
    gym_full_80 = 0.8
    #The answer is
    result = (gym_full_80 - gym_full_60) * people_came_in
    return result

    #There were 12 patients

    monthly_cost = 10
    #If you pay for a year in advance the gym will give you two months free
    free_months = 2
    #A year is 12 months

    #The answer is

    #24 cans of soda cost $5

    #36 cans of soda would cost

    return result

### Response: Question: A 100-liter tank has 50 liters of water. 10 liters of water are added to the tank each day. How many days will it take to fill the tank? Solution: def solution():
    #The tank has 50 liters of water
    water_initial = 50
    #10 liters of water are added each day
    water_added_per_day = 10
    #The tank is 100 liters
    water_tank_size = 100
    #The answer is
    result = (water_tank_size - water_initial) / water_added_per_day
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery sells 24 loaves of bread each day.  Monday through Friday, the bakery sells 24 loaves of bread.  On Saturday, the bakery sells 36 loaves of bread.  How many loaves of bread does the bakery sell in one week? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery sells 24 loaves of bread each day
    loaves_per_day = 24
    #Monday through Friday, the bakery sells 24 loaves of bread
    loaves_monday_friday = loaves_per_day * 5
    #On Saturday, the bakery sells 36 loaves of bread
    loaves_saturday = 36
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_monday_friday + loaves_saturday
    return result

### Response: Question: A 1000-page book has 200 pages of preface and 300 pages of appendices. How many pages of main content does it have? Solution: def solution():
    #The book has 200 pages of preface
    preface_pages = 200
    #and 300 pages of appendices
    appendix_pages = 300
    #The answer is
    result = 1000 - preface_pages - appendix_pages
    return result

### Response: Question: A warehouse has 2500 boxes. They receive 500 more boxes a day, from Monday to Thursday. How many boxes do they have now? Solution: def solution():
    #They have 2500 boxes
    boxes_initial = 2500
    #They receive 500 more boxes a day
    boxes_received_per_day = 500
    #There are 4 days between Monday and Thursday
    num_days = 4
    #They received
    boxes_received = boxes_received_per_day * num_days
    #The answer is
    result = boxes_initial + boxes_received
    return result

    return result

    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon

    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned

### Response: Question: The cafeteria has 200 plates. They wash 50 plates each hour, from 10:00 AM to 1:00 PM. How many plates do they have at 1:00 PM? Solution: def solution():
    #The cafeteria has 200 plates
    plates_initial = 200
    #They wash 50 plates an hour
    plates_washed_per_hour = 50
    #There are 3 hours between 10:00 AM and 1:00 PM
    num_hours = 3
    #They wash
    plates_washed = plates_washed_per_hour * num_hours
    #The answer is
    result = plates_initial - plates_washed
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery sells 100 loaves of bread on Monday. On Tuesday, it sells 50. On Wednesday, it sells 20. On Thursday, it sells 30. On Friday, it sells 40. How many loaves of bread did the bakery sell in a week? Solution: def solution
### Response: Question: A pizza place is selling pizzas for $12.  They have a $2 off coupon.  If you buy 2 pizzas, you get the 2nd pizza for half price.  How much do you pay for 2 pizzas with the coupon? Solution: def solution():
    #A pizza costs $12
    pizza_cost = 12
    #The coupon is for $2 off
    coupon_discount = 2
    #The second pizza is half price
    second_pizza_cost = pizza_cost / 2
    #The answer is
    result = pizza_cost + second_pizza_cost - coupon_discount
    return result

### Response: Question: The bakery has 200 loaves of bread. The bakery sells 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returns 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread does the bakery have left? Solution: def solution():

    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning = 93

    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is

### Response: Question: A 20-foot-long, 10-foot-wide, and 10-foot-tall box is filled with 1000 4-inch-long, 2-inch-wide, and 2-inch-tall boxes. How many 4-inch-long, 2-inch-wide, and 2-inch-tall boxes can fit in the 20-foot-long, 10-foot-wide, and 10-foot-tall box? Solution: def solution():
    #The large box is 20' long
    large_box_length = 20
    #The large box is 10' wide
    large_box_width = 10
    #The large box is 10' tall
    large_box_height = 10
    #The small box is 4" long
    small_box_length = 4
    #The small box is 2" wide
    small_box_width = 2
    #The small box is 2" tall
    small_box_height = 2
    #The large box is 20' long
    large_box_volume = large_box_length * large_box_width * large_box_height
    #The small box is 4" long
    small_box_volume = small_box_length * small_box_width * small_box_height
    #The answer is
    result = large_box_volume / small_box_volume
    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-pound bag of carrots has 120 carrots. A 20-pound bag of onions has 160 onions. A 20-pound bag of potatoes has 240 potatoes. A 20-pound bag of turnips has 280 turnips. What is the average number of vegetables in a 20-pound bag? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-pound bag of carrots has 120 carrots
    carrots_per_bag = 120
    #A 20-pound bag of onions has 160 onions
    onions_per_bag = 160
    #A 20-pound bag of potatoes has 240 potatoes
    potatoes_per_bag = 240
    #A 20-pound bag of turnips has 280 turnips
    turnips_per_bag = 280
    #The total number of vegetables in 20-pound bags is
    total_vegetables = carrots_per_bag + onions_per_bag + potatoes_per_bag + turnips_per_bag
    #The number of 20-pound bags is
    num_bags = 4
    #The average number of vegetables in a 20-pound bag is
    result = total_vegetables / num_bags
    return result

### Response: Question: A 100-page book will take 4 hours to read at a rate of 25 pages per hour. How long will it take to read at a rate of 15 pages per hour? Solution: def solution():
    #A 100-page book will take 4 hours to read at a rate of 25 pages per hour
    book_length = 100
    pages_per_hour = 25
    hours_to_read = book_length / pages_per_hour
    #How long will it take to read at a rate of 15 pages per hour?
    pages_per_hour_slower = 15
    hours_to_read_slower = book_length / pages_per_hour_slower
    #The answer is
    result = hours_to_read_slower
    return result

    #The answer is
    result = towels_total - towels_washing - towels_drying - towels_lost
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery is making 2400 rolls. They have 4 ovens and each oven can bake 150 rolls at a time. How many times do they have to bake the rolls to make 2400? Solution: def solution():

    #Each oven can bake 150 rolls

    #They need to bake 2400 rolls

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are midfielders. The rest of the players are defenders. How many players are defenders? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 are midfielders
    players_midfielders = 6
    #The rest are defenders
    players_defenders = players_total - players_forwards - players_midfielders
    return players_defenders

### Response: Question: The bakery made 200 donuts. They sold 93 donuts in the morning and 39 donuts in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 donuts. How many donuts did they have left? Solution: def solution():

    #The grocery store returned 6 donuts

    #The answer is

### Response: Question: The 4th grade class is 2/3 the size of the 5th grade class.  The 5th grade class is 1/4 the size of the 6th grade class.  The 6th grade class has 24 students.  How many 4th graders are there? Solution: def solution():
    #The 6th grade class has 24 students
    sixth_grade_students = 24
    #The 5th grade class is 1/4 the size of the 6th grade class
    fifth_grade_students = sixth_grade_students / 4
    #The 4th grade class is 2/3 the size of the 5th grade class
    fourth_grade_students = fifth_grade_students * 2 / 3
    return fourth_grade_students

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces.  A bottle of detergent weighs 24 ounces.  A box of bleach weighs 12 ounces.  A bottle of fabric softener weighs 10 ounces.  A 10 pound bag of laundry weighs 160 ounces.  How many ounces of laundry supplies can you buy with a 10 pound bag of laundry? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake = 4
    #A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces
    soap_powder = 16
    #A bottle of detergent weighs 24 ounces
    detergent = 24
    #A box of bleach weighs 12 ounces
    bleach = 12
    #A bottle of fabric softener weighs 10 ounces
    fabric_softener = 10
    #A 10 pound bag of laundry weighs 160 ounces
    laundry = 160
    #The answer is
    result = laundry / (soap_cake + soap_powder + detergent + bleach + fabric_softener)
    return result

### Response: Question: A candy store sells 10000000 pieces of candy a day. On Tuesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy. On Wednesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy.     candy_sold_per_day = 10000000
    #On Tuesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_tuesday = candy_sold_per_day
    #On Wednesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_wednesday = candy_sold_per_day
    #On Thursday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_thursday = candy_sold_per_day
    #On Friday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_friday = candy_sold_per_day
    #The answer is
    result = candy_sold_tuesday + candy_sold_wednesday + candy_sold_thursday + candy_sold_friday
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces. 2 cakes of soap are packaged together. A box of 48 soap cakes is shipped to a warehouse. What is the total weight, in ounces, of the box of soap cakes? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #2 cakes of soap are packaged together
    soap_package_weight = 2 * soap_cake_weight
    #A box of 48 soap cakes is shipped to a warehouse
    soap_cake_box_weight = 48 * soap_package_weight
    #The answer is
    result = soap_cake_box_weight

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakers started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93
    loaves_sold_afternoon=39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-pound box of oranges has 120 oranges. A 5-pound box of oranges has 60 oranges. How many oranges weigh one pound? Solution: def solution():
    #10 pounds of oranges is 120 oranges
    oranges_10_pounds = 120
    #5 pounds of oranges is 60 oranges
    oranges_5_pounds = 60
    #The difference is
    oranges_per_pound = (oranges_10_pounds - oranges_5_pounds) / 5
    return oranges_per_pound

### Response: Question: A bakery makes 200 loaves of bread a day. 40% of the bread is sold in the morning and 60% of the bread is sold in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread are not sold? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery makes 200 loaves of bread a day
    loaves_baked = 200
    #40% of the bread is sold in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked * 0.4
    #60% of the bread is sold in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = loaves_baked * 0.6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A cafeteria in a high school sells 100 hamburgers every day. On Monday, they sold 10 hamburgers. On Tuesday, they sold 20 hamburgers. On Wednesday, they sold 15 hamburgers.     #The cafeteria sells 100 hamburgers a day
    hamburgers_per_day = 100
    #On Monday, they sold 10 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_monday = 10
    #On Tuesday, they sold 20 hamburgers

    #On Wednesday, they sold 15 hamburgers

    #On Thursday, they sold 25 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_thursday = 25
    #On Friday, they sold 30 hamburgers

    result = hamburgers_sold_monday + hamburgers_sold_tuesday + hamburgers_sold_wednesday + hamburgers_sold_thursday + hamburgers_sold_friday
    return result

    #750 of them were from the visiting team

### Response: Question: The cashier at the bakery has $100 in the register. The first customer of the day buys 2 loaves of bread for $3 each. The second customer buys 2 baguettes for $2 each. The third customer buys 1 croissant for $4. The fourth customer buys 1 muffin for $2. How much money does the cashier have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The cashier started with $100
    cashier_money_initial = 100
    #The first customer bought 2 loaves of bread for $3 each
    first_customer_loaves = 2
    first_customer_loaf_cost = 3
    first_customer_money = first_customer_loaves * first_customer_loaf_cost
    #The second customer bought 2 baguettes for $2 each
    second_customer_baguettes = 2
    second_customer_baguette_cost = 2
    second_customer_money = second_customer_baguettes * second_customer_baguette_cost
    #The third customer bought 1 croissant for $4
    third_customer_croissant_cost = 4
    third_customer_money = third_customer_croissant_cost
    #The fourth customer bought 1 muffin for $2
    fourth_customer_muffin_cost = 2
    fourth_customer_money = fourth_customer_muffin_cost
    #The answer is
    result = cashier_money_initial - first_customer_money - second_customer_money - third_customer_money - fourth_customer_money
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery has 12 cakes. The bakery sells 1/3 of the cakes in the morning and 2/3 of the cakes in the afternoon. How many cakes are left at the end of the day? Solution: def solution():

    #1/3 of the cakes are sold in the morning

    #2/3 of the cakes are sold in the afternoon

    #The answer is

    return result

    #The pipe has 20000 liters of water
    water_initial = 20000
    #2000 liters of water are flowing into the pipe every minute
    water_per_minute = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = water_initial / water_per_minute
    return result

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakers started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93
    loaves_sold_afternoon=39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-foot wall is to be built using 4-inch bricks. How many bricks are needed to build the wall? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-foot wall is 20 * 12 = <<20*12=240>>240 inches
    wall_length = 240
    #A 4-inch brick is 4/12 = 1/3 of a foot
    brick_length = 1/3
    #240 inches / 4 inches = <<240/4=60>>60 bricks
    result = wall_length / brick_length
    return result

### Response: Question: A pizzaiolo is making pizzas. He has 12 pizzas in the oven. He can bake 4 pizzas at a time and it takes 15 minutes to bake each pizza. How long will it take to bake all 12 pizzas? Solution: def solution():
    #He can bake 4 pizzas at a time
    pizzas_per_batch = 4
    #It takes 15 minutes to bake a pizza
    minutes_per_pizza = 15
    #He has 12 pizzas
    pizzas_total = 12
    #He will need to bake
    num_batches = pizzas_total / pizzas_per_batch
    #batches of pizza. The answer is
    result = num_batches * minutes_per_pizza
    return result

### Response: Question: 12 bakers baked 200 loaves of bread. 1/4 of the loaves were sold in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining loaves were sold in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread were not sold? Solution: def solution():
    #12 bakers baked 200 loaves of bread
    loaves_baked = 200
    #1/4 of the loaves were sold in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked / 4
    #1/2 of the remaining loaves were sold in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = (loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-foot-long and 12-foot-wide room is to be divided into two equal-sized rooms. What is the perimeter of each new room? Solution: def solution():
    #The original room is 10 feet long
    long_side = 10
    #and 12 feet wide
    short_side = 12
    #The perimeter of the original room is 2 * (long side) + 2 * (short side)
    perimeter_original = 2 * long_side + 2 * short_side
    #The new rooms are half the size, so the perimeter is
    perimeter_new = perimeter_original / 2
    return perimeter_new

### Response: Question: The gym has 200 towels. On Monday, 30 towels are washed. On Tuesday, 50 towels are washed. On Wednesday, 40 towels are washed. On Thursday, 20 towels are washed. On Friday, 30 towels are washed. How many towels are there at the end of Friday? Solution: def solution():
    #The gym started with 200 towels
    towels_initial = 200
    #On Monday, 30 towels were washed
    towels_washed_monday = 30
    #On Tuesday, 50 towels were washed
    towels_washed_tuesday = 50
    #On Wednesday, 40 towels were washed
    towels_washed_wednesday = 40
    #On Thursday, 20 towels were washed
    towels_washed_thursday = 20
    #On Friday, 30 towels were washed
    towels_washed_friday = 30
    #The answer is
    result = towels_initial - towels_washed_monday - towels_washed_tuesday - towels_washed_wednesday - towels_washed_thursday - towels_washed_friday
    return result

    #It sells 93 loaves

    #It has 7 loaves left at the end of the day

    return result

### Response: Question: The gym has 200 towels. On Monday, 32 towels are washed. On Tuesday, 58 towels are washed. On Wednesday, 26 towels are washed. On Thursday, 44 towels are washed. On Friday, 12 towels are washed. How many towels are left unwashed? Solution: def solution():
    #The gym started with 200 towels
    towels_initial = 200
    #On Monday, 32 towels were washed
    towels_washed_monday = 32
    #On Tuesday, 58 towels were washed
    towels_washed_tuesday = 58
    #On Wednesday, 26 towels were washed
    towels_washed_wednesday = 26
    #On Thursday, 44 towels were washed
    towels_washed_thursday = 44
    #On Friday, 12 towels were washed
    towels_washed_friday = 12
    #The total number of towels washed is
    towels_washed_total = towels_washed_monday + towels_washed_tuesday + towels_washed_wednesday + towels_washed_thursday + towels_washed_friday
    #The answer is
    result = towels_initial - towels_washed_total
    return result

### Response: Question: 123456789 is a 9-digit number. If you remove the last digit, the number is divisible by 9. What is the sum of all the digits in the number? Solution: def solution():
    #The number is 123456789
    number = 123456789
    #If you remove the last digit, the number is divisible by 9
    number_no_last_digit = number // 10
    #The sum of the digits is
    result = sum(int(digit) for digit in str(number_no_last_digit))
    return result

    #The 2020 census found 20% more people
    people_2020_increase = 0.2
    #The answer is
    result = people_2010 * (1 + people_2020_increase) - people
### Response: Question: A soccer team has 25 players. 15 of the players are from the United States. 6 of the players are from Mexico. 4 of the players are from Canada. How many players are not from North America? Solution: def solution():
    #A soccer team has 25 players

    #15 of the players are from the United States
    players_usa = 15
    #6 of the players are from Mexico
    players_mexico = 6
    #4 of the players are from Canada
    players_canada = 4
    #The answer is
    result = players_total - players_usa - players_mexico - players_canada
    return result
